Rarely ever to I feel morally obligated to provide any particular title, but this is one of the exceptions. Out of the Shadows is psychoanalisis of what it means to be a gay man in modern America. The author derrives most of this information from personal research as a clinical psychologist. It's great! Two caveats: It's a bit dense. So it won't be accessible to all of our readers, but I'm confident that most who would pick up a book like this will be able to follow along just fine. Also, the topic is heavy. Sex is discussed in a very clinical sense, but the book is not about sex. Added
